quest.name,Eyes behind the Mirror
quest.authors_short,Anton Timmermans
quest.authors,"Created by: <i>Anton Timmermans</i> and <i>William van den Broek</i>\n\nVoiceover by: <i>Stephen Weese</i>"
quest.description,|||<i>The Silver Twilight Lodge strikes back! Too many attempts to shift the balance of power have been foiled by paranormal investigators. High time to teach those pesky investigators a lesson and ensure they never interfere again.</i>\n\nThis scenario includes a substantial amount of battle and light puzzle challenges. An excellent opportunity to get to know the heroic investigators (and their backgrounds) a little better.\nThe maximum board size for this scenario is 2 by 2.5 square tiles.\n\nA scenario for Mansions of Madness 2nd Edition. This scenario can be played with the base game.\nAll expansions or figure & tile collections will provide extra variation (and a bit more difficulty). Expansions "Streets of Arkham" and "Horrific Journeys" add additional layouts for the end game.\n\nAnother endgame layout will come available with future updates of this scenario for expansion "Path of the Serpent".|||
quest.synopsys,Just because you're paranoid, does not mean they're not out to get you.

UIIntroductionText.uitext,|||<align="left">An unexpected sound wakes you from your afternoon nap. As you rise from your comfortable chair, all you hear is the sound of footsteps running away from your door, splashing in puddles of water from this morning's torrential rain.\n\nWhen you turn your attention to the front door, you see a piece of paper peeking out from underneath it. Though the paper is wet from the rain, you manage to pull it out in one piece.\n\nIn the pale candlelight you discover it is a letter addressed to you, but without a sender. The message, ominously composed of letters cut from a newspaper, reads:</align>\n\n<i>"Cease your paranormal investigations and do not interfere with our organization again or suffer the same fate as your friend."</i>|||
UIIntroductionContinueText.uitext,{qst:CONTINUE}
UIIntroduction2Text.uitext,|||<align="left">Worried about which unfortunate friend the writer is referring to, you start to contact all fellow investigators known to you. A few reply, confirming they also received a similar threat. You jointly agree that someone must be in grave danger and action must be taken without delay.\n\nYour suspicions unanimously point towards the Silver Twilight Lodge. This corrupted organization must be responsible for abducting one of your friends who will, most likely, be sacrificed during some horrible ritual.\n\nAfter comparing notes, you decide that the best place to start the investigation is an alleged hideout, a supposedly abandoned estate in the woods, just outside of Arkham.</align>|||

Overwhelmed by the instant boost, they begin to jeer energetically.\n\nAllowing the cultists to get adjusted, the high priest then lights an incense burner upon which the area around the dinosaur skeleton quickly starts to fill with a thick and heavy crimson smoke. Fortunately, the torture cage dangles high enough above it, as such your captured friend is not yet affected by it.\n\nPlace six {qst:CCYAN}Fire Tokens{qst:COFF} in the spaces around the dinosaur skeleton as indicated. These tokens represent the <b>suffocating mist</b>. (Click any fire token for special rules).|||
